architecture:\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\n1. **Standalone Vite App** (`/workspace/`): Source code (`.tsx`, `.ts`, etc.)\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\n2. **Next.js App** (`/workspace/dfp-neo-platform/`): Serves static files from `public/flight-school-app/`\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\n\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\nRailway serves the **pre-built static assets** from `public/flight-school-app/assets/`. When you modify source files in `/workspace/`, you must rebuild the standalone app to regenerate these assets.\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\n\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\n### Solution\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\n\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\nWhen modifying source files in `/workspace/`:\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\n\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\n```bash\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\n# 1. When you modify source files in `/workspace/`, you must rebuild the standalone app to regenerate these assets.\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\n   \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\n   ### Solution\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\n   \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\n   When modifying source files in `/workspace/`:\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\n   \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\n   ```bash\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\n   # 1. Copy new build artifacts to Next.js public directory\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\n   cp -r /workspace/dist/* /workspace/dfp-neo-platform/public/flight-school-app/\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\n   \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\n   # 5. **Direct bundled file changes work immediately** (e.g., modifying `dfp-neo-platform/public/flight-school-app/assets/*.js` directly)\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\n   - **Source file changes don\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\'t work** unless the standalone app is rebuilt and new bundles are copied to the public directory\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\n   \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\n   ### Why This Happens\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\n   \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\n   The application has a two-part architecture:\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\n   1. **Standalone Vite App** (`/workspace/`): Source code (`.tsx`, `.ts`, etc.)\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\n   2. **Next.js App** (`/workspace/dfp-neo-platform/`): Serves static files from `public/flight-school-app/`\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\n   \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\n   Railway serves the **pre-built static assets** from `public/flight-school-app/assets/`. When you modify source files in `/workspace/`, you must rebuild the standalone app to regenerate these assets.\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\n   \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\n   ### Solution\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\n   \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\n   When modifying source files in `/workspace/`:\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\n   \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\n   ```bash\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\n   # 1. Navigate to standalone app directory\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\n   cd /workspace\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\n   \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\n   # 2. Install dependencies (if needed)\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\n   npm install\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\n   \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\n   # 3. Build the standalone app\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\n   npm run build\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\n   \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\n   # 4. Copy new build artifacts to Next.js public directory\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\n   cp -r /workspace/dist/* /workspace/dfp-neo-platform/public/flight-school-app/\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\n   \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\n   # 5. Verify the changes are in the bundled files\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\n   # Example: Check if \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"Staff Database\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\" appears in bundled JavaScript\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\n   grep -o \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"Staff Database\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\" /workspace/dfp-neo-platform/public/flight-school-app/assets/*.js | wc -l\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\n   \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\n   # 6. Commit and push changes\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\n   cd /workspace\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\n   git add dfp-neo-platform/public/flight-school-app/\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\n   git commit -m \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"feat: [description] - Rebuilt standalone app to include latest source changes\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\n   git push\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\n   ```\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\n   \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\n   ### Key Points\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\n   \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\n   - **Modify source files** \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\u2192 MUST rebuild using `npm run build`\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\n   - **Modify bundled files directly** \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\u2192 NO build needed, but not recommended\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\n   - Always verify changes appear in the bundled JavaScript files before committing\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\n   - The build output goes to `/workspace/dist/` and must be copied to `public/flight-school-app/`\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\n   \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\n   ### When to Use This Solution\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\n   \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\n   - Adding new components or features to the standalone app\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\n   - Modifying React components (`.tsx` files)\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\n   - Changing TypeScript source code\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\n   -
